<gmapID>0x80dc72e5b25eaaab:0x2a6adb09c97fe8c5</gmapID>< Text>
Travel Transparency in itself is a cool business idea. They do require an up-front cost, ranging from $3k - $10k, to basically give you membership and access to discounted hotels, time shares, houses etc. . . Sometimes the price for a full week (for a hotel or time share) is around $200. This is an insanely good deal.

There's a yearly fee of $150, and if there wasn't a $3k initial investment my wife and I would have jumped on it. This private membership does offer some great prices on vacations. So the initial investment ($3k - $10k) could make A LOT of sense, and save you a lot of money if you're going to travel a good amount.

My issue is mostly with their marketing company. They got my wife and I to show up. So kudos to that. They did their job. But we asked several times about the details of the "round trip airfare". We were told we won free tickets from Delta and could fly anywhere in the continental US. We asked about restrictions and the marketing company said we would receive an email with all details. The email we got just further highlighted that we would get 2 round trip tickets and 2 nights in a hotel! Sounds great right? **Terms and conditions apply** But they do charge $75/person in gov't fees and $75/person in a "reservation fee". We thought, "ok, if we can fly from San Diego to New York for $150/person, that's still pretty good". Because of this, we went through the presentation, which was well done. Very nice people. No complaints in the presentation. I just wish they would have told us about the flight restrictions up front.

After the presentation we get our "voucher" for the plane tickets:

**Valid for Monday, Tuesday or Wednesday Departure dates only**
**you are required to send $100 cashiers check to CasablancaExpress to request your travel dates**
** The $100 cashiers check is refundable 30 days AFTER you complete your travel**
**After Casablanca gets your $100 cashiers check. They send you a reservation letter that you must complete with your requested departure dates. You must send this back with $75/person reservation fee**
**You must provide THREE different departure dates at least 60 days in advance of your first date and 30 days between subsequent dates**
**You must provide at least one alternate destination**
**All reservations are subject to availability**

These last few qualifications makes planning a trip really hard. This makes me assume that CasablancaExpress (who you're sending $100 to, then $75/person to) gets to pick any of the 3 dates (within a 3 month range) that you provided, and either to your preferred destination OR the backup destination?? I'm assuming they will just pick the worst/cheapest date, and the cheaper destination.

Departing flights are between 3-10 and return flights are between 6am - 1.

Your tickets will be mailed at least 10 days prior to your arrival date. . .

All of this would have been good to know BEFORE agreeing to the meeting. This is what should have been provided in the email. I understand that Travel Transparency can kinda blame this on "their marketing companies" But if they don't know what their marketing companies are telling their future customers, theres a little bit of blame on Travel Transparency for that. . .

For a company called travel TRANSPARENCY, this was not a good start to doing business with them.

The flight/hotel deal has wayyy too many *send me money first by mail cashiers check* *send me more money by mail with 3 different dates that they get to choose* -- WAY TOO COMPLICATED for a company who is trying to make travel easier by just going online and booking a vacation. I feel like their promotion should be in-line with their business model. Not something that will be extremely hard to plan around (what am I suppose to ask my boss for 3 different travel dates for 3 subsequent months and be like "yeah boss sorry, I'm going on a vacation, but i dont know when yet, can i get march 3-7, april 3-7 and May 3-7 off please?".)

I wish the business success because I like the business model. They need to change their marketing plan</Text>

I, like everyone else it seems, am trying to find a handgun and also a rifle. I was getting set to join the club to go shooting because they have perks for members. The range was okay, seemed typical for a few that I have been to over the years which isn't many but it doesn't take a whole lot to figure it out.
The staff however is a bit on the 'pithy' side. Two or maybe three conversations on the phone left me not feeling like I want to join. Mind you, it is a financial commitment, aka, not cheap.
On the positive note, the help at the range was good. At least, the one time I was there. I will continue to shop as the California legislature makes it impossible to shoot or buy ammo. Too bad the service didn't leave me with the feeling of wanting to get more serious. On the other hand, maybe it is better off. I will use my cell phone for help and then throw my phone at the perpetrator.< /Review>

<review>Worst experience I have ever had with any property mangament company!!!! From the rental property to the customer service this business is by far the worst business.

I have only been in this rental property house for 6 days and I have numerous incidents and issues already.

This high end rental house ($4400 per month) was advertised as "move in ready" which clearly was not move in ready. The day I moved in I found out the refrigerator was broken and a new one was to be delivered the next day. I drove 4 hours to get here and I had groceries that needed to be refrigerated. I ended up throwing 3 large bags of food away. The communication was very poor from Mangold Property Management. If they knew the refrigerator was broken the day before I came they could have called/emailed me and informed me that a the refrigerator was broken, a new one was coming in a couple of days and not to pack any perishable items for there is no place to store them. I could have given my 3 bags of food away rather than packing it and letting it spoil.

Besides the broken refrigerator there was no microwave in the kitchen. 6 days ago when I signed my lease I was told a microwave should be coming but they had no clue when it is suppose to get here. 6 days later and still no word on the microwave.

Dennis the owner of Mangold Property also told me that the place would have a full clean from top to bottom before we moved in. That was not the case. In the master bathroom, old urine was clearly visible around the bottom base of the toilet. The carpets were so old and the smell was so bad it made me nauseous. We called Mangold Property and they sent someone to wash the carpet which was nice, but this should have been taken care of before we moved in.

The bedrooms are all upstairs and the 2 bedrooms where my kids sleep are connected to an outdoor balcony. The balcony doors in both bedrooms do not lock which seem like a serious safety issue. My kids are 3 and 5 and I do not want them having free access to a 2nd story balcony. I temporarily solved this issue by placing both of their dressers in front of the balcony door preventing the door from swinging open.

There were also these old armoires that are broken, wobbly, and tilting heavily to one side that could have been a disaster if it fell. They weren't attached to the wall and the most of the pieces were all broken. The have removed one of them to the garage and their still is one more upstairs that needs to be removed.

The oven had a broken knob so we could not turn the oven on. STEVE from the Mangold Property was sent to my rental to do an initial inspection today. He figured that we would not use the griddle as often so he removed that knob and placed it where the broken oven knob was. The knobs have different numbers on them so that quick fix did not work. It actually just filled the house with gas. I mentioned to him that the whole house smelled like gas now and he replied, "I don't smell anything". < Review>
This is a clean, well-managed place convenient to everything yet tucked away on a quiet out-of-the-way street. I felt reassured with my four wheeled family heirloom in storage there. Never had a problem with access, and the facility is extremely safe. Ken, the current manager, took a personal interest in my needs and security.

Extra Space offered the best rates initially - but the gradual increases really started to make this place unaffordable. Over three years the rent increased nearly 75% - while my salary increased by 0%. Had I not had other arrangements, I would have started to look for alternatives. That being said, this Extra Space is still a great place for short-term storage.< /Review>
